# Empire Capital-Megaplex
building_novus_machine_capital_4 = {
	base_buildtime = 1200
	is_listed = no
	icon = "building_novus_capital_4"
	planet_unique = yes
	capital = yes
	level = 4
	cost = { minerals = 1500 }
	produced_resources = {
		energy = 10
		unity = 3
	}
	produced_resource_trigger = {
		modifier = {
			has_non_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever
			has_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever_machine
			has_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever_hive
			resources = { unity = 1 }
		}
	}
	adjacency_bonus = {
		tile_building_resource_minerals_add = 4
		tile_building_resource_energy_add = 4
	}
	show_tech_unlock_if = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
	potential = {
		owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
		}
	}
	destroy_if = {
		exists = owner
		owner = {
			NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
		}
	}
	upgrades = { building_novus_machine_capital_5 }
	prerequisites = { "tech_novus_stellar_administration" }
	ai_replace = no
}
# Empire Capital-Superplex
building_novus_machine_capital_5 = {
	base_buildtime = 1500
	is_listed = no
	icon = "building_novus_capital_5"
	planet_unique = yes
	capital = yes
	level = 5
	cost = {
		minerals = 2000
		influence = 150
	}
	produced_resources = {
		energy = 12
		unity = 4
		influence = 1
	}
	produced_resource_trigger = {
		modifier = {
			has_non_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever
			has_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever_machine
			has_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever_hive
			resources = { unity = 1 }
		}
	}
	adjacency_bonus = {
		tile_building_resource_minerals_add = 5
		tile_building_resource_energy_add = 5
	}
	show_tech_unlock_if = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
	potential = {
		owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
		}
	}
	destroy_if = {
		exists = owner
		owner = {
			NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
		}
	}
	prerequisites = { "tech_novus_stellar_administration" }
	ai_replace = no
}

# Grand Mausoleum
building_novus_grand_mausoleum = {
	base_buildtime = 360
	planet_unique = yes
	cost = { minerals = 200 }
	planet_modifier = { pop_government_ethic_attraction = 0.05 }
	potential = {
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
		}
	}
	allow = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_building_capital_2"
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_building_capital_2 = yes
						has_building_capital_3 = yes
						has_building_novus_capital_4 = yes
						has_building_novus_capital_5 = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_building_machine_capital_2"
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_building_machine_capital_2 = yes
						has_building = "building_machine_capital_3"
						has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_4"
						has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_5"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	ai_weight = { weight = 10 }
	prerequisites = { "tech_novus_grand_mausoleum" }
	ai_allow = {
		NOR = {
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_betharian
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_geode_deposit
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_enriched_soil
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_alien_pets
				amount > 0
			}
		}
	}
}
building_novus_planetary_park = {
	base_buildtime = 360
	empire_unique = yes
	icon = "building_novus_planetary_park"
	cost = {
		minerals = 100
		energy = 75
	}
	required_resources = {
		energy = 1
		minerals = 1
	}
	produced_resources = {
		society_research = 2
		food = 1
	}
	country_modifier = { pop_happiness = 0.05 }
	potential = {
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
		}
	}
	allow = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_building_capital_1_or_hab"
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_building_capital_1 = yes
						has_building_capital_2 = yes
						has_building_capital_3 = yes
						has_building_novus_capital_4 = yes
						has_building_novus_capital_5 = yes
						has_building = "building_hab_capital"
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_building_machine_capital_1_or_hab"
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_building_machine_capital_1 = yes
						has_building_machine_capital_2 = yes
						has_building = "building_machine_capital_3"
						has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_4"
						has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_5"
						has_building = "building_hab_capital"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	ai_weight = {
		factor = 10000
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			from = {
				count_pops = {
					count < 12
					limit = { is_colony_pop = yes }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	prerequisites = { "tech_novus_planetary_park" }
	ai_allow = {
		NOR = {
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_betharian
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_geode_deposit
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_enriched_soil
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_alien_pets
				amount > 0
			}
		}
	}
}

building_novus_virtual_combat_arena = {
	base_buildtime = 360
	planet_unique = yes
	cost = { minerals = 350 }
	required_resources = { energy = 3 }
	planet_modifier = {
		pop_happiness = 0.05
		pop_government_ethic_attraction = 0.05
	}
	army_modifier = { army_damage_mult = 0.10 }
	allow = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_building_capital_1"
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_building_capital_1 = yes
						has_building_capital_2 = yes
						has_building_capital_3 = yes
						has_building_novus_capital_4 = yes
						has_building_novus_capital_5 = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_building_machine_capital_1"
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_building_machine_capital_1 = yes
						has_building_machine_capital_2 = yes
						has_building = "building_machine_capital_3"
						has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_4"
						has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_5"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	prerequisites = { "tech_novus_virtual_combat_arena" }
	ai_weight = {
		weight = 1000
		modifier = {
			weight = 0
			from = {
				happiness_planet > 0.90
				NOT = { has_building = building_novus_virtual_combat_arena }
			}
		}
	}
	ai_weight = { weight = 10 }
	ai_allow = {
		NOR = {
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_betharian
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_geode_deposit
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_enriched_soil
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_alien_pets
				amount > 0
			}
		}
	}
}
#Battle Training Center
building_novus_battle_training_center = {
	base_buildtime = 720
	empire_unique = yes
	icon = "building_novus_battle_training_center"
	cost = {
		minerals = 300
		influence = 50
	}
	required_resources = { energy = 3 }
	potential = {
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
		}
	}
	allow = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_any_empire_capital"
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_building_capital_3 = yes
						has_building_novus_capital_4 = yes
						has_building_novus_capital_5 = yes
						has_building = "building_hab_capital"
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_any_machine_empire_capital"
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_building = "building_machine_capital_3"
						has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_4"
						has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_5"
						has_building = "building_hab_capital"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	planet_modifier = { planet_army_build_speed_mult = 0.35 }
	army_modifier = { army_morale = 0.10 }
	produced_resources = { society_research = 2 }
	prerequisites = { "tech_novus_battle_training_center" }
	ai_weight = { weight = 10000 }
	ai_allow = {
		NOR = {
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_betharian
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_geode_deposit
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_enriched_soil
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_alien_pets
				amount > 0
			}
		}
	}
}

			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
		}

			limit = {

					}
				}

			limit = {
				owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
			}
			custom_tooltip = {

			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_enriched_soil
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_alien_pets
				amount > 0
			}
		}
	}
}

# Empire Capital-Megaplex
building_novus_capital_4_direct_build = {
	base_buildtime = 2610
	icon = "building_novus_capital_4"
	planet_unique = yes
	capital = yes
	level = 4
	cost = { minerals = 3350 }
	planet_modifier = { pop_government_ethic_attraction = 0.20 }
	produced_resource_trigger = {
		modifier = {
			OR = {
				has_non_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever
				has_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever_machine
				has_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever_hive
			}
			resources = { unity = 1 }
		}
	}
	produced_resources = {
		energy = 10
		unity = 3
	}
	potential = {
		NOT = {
			owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
		}
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
		}
		NOT = {
			tile = { has_building_novus_capital_4 = yes }
		}
		NAND = {
			owner = { has_technology = "tech_novus_stellar_administration" }
			NOT = {
				owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
			}
			planet = {
				NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			}
			owner = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = display_low_tier_flag  }
			}
		}
	}
	destroy_if = {
		exists = owner
		owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
	}
	adjacency_bonus = {
		tile_building_resource_minerals_add = 4
		tile_building_resource_food_add = 4
		tile_building_resource_energy_add = 4
	}
	upgrades = { building_novus_capital_5 }
	prerequisites = { "tech_novus_stellar_administration" }
	ai_replace = no
	show_tech_unlock_if = { always = no }
}

building_novus_diplomatic_center_1 = {
	icon = "building_novus_diplomatic_center_1"
	empire_unique = yes
	base_buildtime = 360
	cost = { minerals = 350 }
	required_resources = { energy = 3 }
	produced_resources = { influence = 0.25 }
	country_modifier = { max_influence = 100 }
	prerequisites = { "tech_planetary_government" }
	upgrades = { building_novus_diplomatic_center_2 }
	potential = {
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
		}
	}
	allow = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_building_capital_1"
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_building_capital_1 = yes
						has_building_capital_2 = yes
						has_building_capital_3 = yes
						has_building_novus_capital_4 = yes
						has_building_novus_capital_5 = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_building_machine_capital_1"
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_building_machine_capital_1 = yes
						has_building_machine_capital_2 = yes
						has_building = "building_machine_capital_3"
						has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_4"
						has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_5"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	ai_allow = {
		NOR = {
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_betharian
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_geode_deposit
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_enriched_soil
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_alien_pets
				amount > 0
			}
		}
	}
	ai_weight = { weight = 5000 }
}

		shipsize_colonizer_build_cost_mult = -0.15
		pop_environment_tolerance = 0.05
	}
	potential = {
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
		}
		owner = { has_tradition = tr_expansion_finish }
	}
	allow = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_building_novus_capital_5"
				planet = { has_building_novus_capital_5 = yes }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_building_novus_machine_capital_5"
				planet = { has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_5" }
			}
		}
	}
	ai_weight = { weight = 10000 }
}

	base_buildtime = 667
	planet_unique = yes
	icon = "building_novus_power_hub_3"
	cost = { minerals = 460 }
	potential = {
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
		}
		NOT = {
			tile = { has_building_novus_power_hub_3 = yes }
		}
		NAND = {
			owner = { has_technology = "tech_novus_power_hub_4" }
			planet = {
				NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = "requires_building_capital_3"
					planet = {
						OR = {
							has_building_capital_3 = yes
							has_building_novus_capital_4 = yes
							has_building_novus_capital_5 = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
				}
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = "requires_building_machine_capital_3"
					planet = {
						OR = {
							has_building = "building_machine_capital_3"
							has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_4"
							has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_5"
						}
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip_fail = {
				fail_text = "requires_power_hub_absence"
				planet = {
					NOT = { has_building = "building_akx_worm_1" }
				}
			}
			owner = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = display_low_tier_flag  }
			}
		}
	}
	produced_resource_trigger = {
		modifier = {
			has_tradition = tr_prosperity_pursuit_of_profit
			resources = { unity = 2 }
		}
	}
	allow = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_building_capital_2"
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_building_capital_2 = yes
						has_building_capital_3 = yes
						has_building_novus_capital_4 = yes
						has_building_novus_capital_5 = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_building_machine_capital_2"
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_building_machine_capital_2 = yes
						has_building = "building_machine_capital_3"
						has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_4"
						has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_5"
					}
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip_fail = {
			fail_text = "requires_power_hub_absence"
			planet = {
				NOT = { has_building = "building_akx_worm_1" }
			}
		}
	}
	produced_resources = { energy = 6 }
	planet_modifier = { tile_resource_energy_mult = 0.15 }
	upgrades = { building_novus_power_hub_4 }
	prerequisites = { "tech_novus_power_hub_3" }
	ai_allow = {
		NOR = {
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_betharian
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_alien_pets
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_geode_deposit
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_enriched_soil
				amount > 0
			}
		}
	}
	ai_weight = {
		factor = 10
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			is_slave_tile_or_planet = yes
		}
	}
	show_tech_unlock_if = { always = no }
}

building_novus_power_hub_4_direct_build = {
	base_buildtime = 937
	planet_unique = yes
	icon = "building_novus_power_hub_4"
	cost = { minerals = 740 }
	potential = {
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
		}
		NOT = {
			tile = { has_building_novus_power_hub_4 = yes }
		}
		NAND = {
			owner = { has_technology = "tech_novus_power_hub_5" }
			planet = {
				NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = "requires_building_novus_capital_4"
					planet = {
						OR = {
							has_building_novus_capital_4 = yes
							has_building_novus_capital_5 = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
				}
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = "requires_building_novus_machine_capital_4"
					planet = {
						OR = {
							has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_4"
							has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_5"
						}
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip_fail = {
				fail_text = "requires_power_hub_absence"
				planet = {
					NOT = { has_building = "building_akx_worm_1" }
				}
			}
			owner = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = display_low_tier_flag  }
			}
		}
	}
	produced_resource_trigger = {
		modifier = {
			has_tradition = tr_prosperity_pursuit_of_profit
			resources = { unity = 2 }
		}
	}
	allow = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_building_capital_3"
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_building_capital_3 = yes
						has_building_novus_capital_4 = yes
						has_building_novus_capital_5 = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_building_machine_capital_3"
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_building = "building_machine_capital_3"
						has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_4"
						has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_5"
					}
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip_fail = {
			fail_text = "requires_power_hub_absence"
			planet = {
				NOT = { has_building = "building_akx_worm_1" }
			}
		}
	}
	produced_resources = { energy = 8 }
	planet_modifier = { tile_resource_energy_mult = 0.20 }
	upgrades = { building_novus_power_hub_5 }
	prerequisites = { "tech_novus_power_hub_4" }
	ai_allow = {
		NOR = {
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_betharian
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_alien_pets
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_geode_deposit
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_enriched_soil
				amount > 0
			}
		}
	}
	ai_weight = {
		factor = 10
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			is_slave_tile_or_planet = yes
		}
	}
	show_tech_unlock_if = { always = no }
}

			fail_text = "requires_power_hub_absence"

				NOT = { has_building = "building_akx_worm_1" }
			}
		}
	}
	produced_resources = { energy = 8 }
	planet_modifier = { tile_resource_energy_mult = 0.20 }
	upgrades = { building_novus_power_hub_5 }
	prerequisites = { "tech_novus_power_hub_4" }

				type = sr_novus_enriched_soil
				amount > 0
			}

				type = sr_alien_pets
				amount > 0
			}
		}
	}
	ai_weight = {
		factor = 10
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			is_slave_tile_or_planet = yes
		}

#####################################################
# Geode Mining Networks

building_novus_geode_mining_network_1 = {
	base_buildtime = @b1time
	icon = "building_novus_geode_mining_network_1"
	cost = { minerals = @b1cost }
	required_resources = { energy = 1 }
	potential = {
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
		}
		NAND = {
			owner = { has_technology = "tech_mining_network_2" }
			planet = {
				NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = "requires_building_capital_2"
					planet = {
						OR = {
							has_building_capital_2 = yes
							has_building_capital_3 = yes
							has_building_novus_capital_4 = yes
							has_building_novus_capital_5 = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
				}
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = "requires_building_machine_capital_2"
					planet = {
						OR = {
							has_building_machine_capital_2 = yes
							has_building = "building_machine_capital_3"
							has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_4"
							has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_5"
						}
					}
				}
			}
			owner = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = display_low_tier_flag  }
			}
		}
	}
	allow = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_building_capital_1"
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_building_capital_1 = yes
						has_building_capital_2 = yes
						has_building_capital_3 = yes
						has_building_novus_capital_4 = yes
						has_building_novus_capital_5 = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_building_machine_capital_1"
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_building_machine_capital_1 = yes
						has_building_machine_capital_2 = yes
						has_building = "building_machine_capital_3"
						has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_4"
						has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_5"
					}
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip_fail = {
			fail_text = "requires_geode_deposit"
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = sr_novus_geode_deposit
					amount > 0
				}
			}
		}
	}
	produced_resources = { minerals = 6 }
	prerequisites = { "tech_novus_mine_geode_deposit" }
	upgrades = { building_novus_geode_mining_network_2 }
	ai_weight = { weight = 100 }
}

	base_buildtime = 667
	planet_unique = yes
	icon = "building_novus_mineral_processing_plant_3"
	cost = { minerals = 460 }
	potential = {
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
		}
		NOT = {
			tile = { has_building_novus_mineral_processing_plant_3 = yes }
		}
		NAND = {
			owner = { has_technology = "tech_novus_mineral_processing_4" }
			planet = {
				NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = "requires_building_capital_3"
					planet = {
						OR = {
							has_building_capital_3 = yes
							has_building_novus_capital_4 = yes
							has_building_novus_capital_5 = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
				}
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = "requires_building_machine_capital_3"
					planet = {
						OR = {
							has_building = "building_machine_capital_3"
							has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_4"
							has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_5"
						}
					}
				}
			}
			owner = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = display_low_tier_flag  }
			}
		}
	}
	allow = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_building_capital_2"
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_building_capital_2 = yes
						has_building_capital_3 = yes
						has_building_novus_capital_4 = yes
						has_building_novus_capital_5 = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_building_machine_capital_2"
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_building_machine_capital_2 = yes
						has_building = "building_machine_capital_3"
						has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_4"
						has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_5"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	produced_resources = { minerals = 6 }
	planet_modifier = { tile_resource_minerals_mult = 0.15 }
	required_resources = { energy = 4 }
	upgrades = { building_novus_mineral_processing_plant_4 }
	prerequisites = { "tech_novus_mineral_processing_3" }
	ai_weight = { weight = 10 }
	ai_allow = {
		NOR = {
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_betharian
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_alien_pets
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_geode_deposit
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_enriched_soil
				amount > 0
			}
		}
	}
	show_tech_unlock_if = { always = no }
}

	base_buildtime = @b1time
	icon = "building_novus_enriched_farm_1"
	cost = { minerals = @b1cost }
	required_resources = { energy = 1 }
	potential = {
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
		}
		NAND = {
			owner = { has_technology = "tech_hydroponics" }
			planet = {
				NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = "requires_building_capital_1"
					planet = {
						OR = {
							has_building_capital_1 = yes
							has_building_capital_2 = yes
							has_building_capital_3 = yes
							has_building_novus_capital_4 = yes
							has_building_novus_capital_5 = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
				}
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = "requires_building_machine_capital_1"
					planet = {
						OR = {
							has_building_machine_capital_1 = yes
							has_building_machine_capital_2 = yes
							has_building = "building_machine_capital_3"
							has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_4"
							has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_5"
						}
					}
				}
			}
			owner = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = display_low_tier_flag  }
			}
		}
	}
	allow = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_building_capital_1"
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_building_capital_1 = yes
						has_building_capital_2 = yes
						has_building_capital_3 = yes
						has_building_novus_capital_4 = yes
						has_building_novus_capital_5 = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_building_machine_capital_1"
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_building_machine_capital_1 = yes
						has_building_machine_capital_2 = yes
						has_building = "building_machine_capital_3"
						has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_4"
						has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_5"
					}
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip_fail = {
			fail_text = "requires_enriched_soil"
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = sr_novus_enriched_soil
					amount > 0
				}
			}
		}
	}
	produced_resources = { food = 6 }

			}

				amount > 0
			}
		}

	}
	ai_weight = { weight = 5000 }

				}

				NOT = { has_building = "building_novus_atmosphere_filtration_plant_1" }

			fail_text = "requires_atmospheric_plant_absence"

				amount > 0

			}

			}

				amount > 0

		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_machine_shelter"
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_building = "building_deployment_post"
						has_building_machine_capital_1 = yes
						has_building_machine_capital_2 = yes
						has_building = "building_machine_capital_3"
						has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_4"
						has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_5"
					}
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip_fail = {
			fail_text = "requires_atmospheric_plant_absence"
			planet = {
				NOT = { has_building = "building_novus_atmosphere_filtration_plant_1" }
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip_fail = {
			fail_text = "requires_atmospheric_plant_absence"
			planet = {
				NOT = { has_building = "building_novus_atmosphere_processing_plant_1" }
			}
		}
	}
	prerequisites = { "tech_novus_atmosphere_processing" }
	ai_allow = {
		NOR = {
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_betharian
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_geode_deposit
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_enriched_soil
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_alien_pets
				amount > 0
			}
			has_building = "building_novus_atmosphere_filtration_plant_1"
			has_building = "building_novus_atmosphere_processing_plant_1"
		}
	}

				amount > 0

## Slave Brainwashing Facility
building_novus_slave_brainwashing_facility_direct_build = {
	base_buildtime = 675
	planet_unique = yes
	cost = { minerals = 650 }
	produced_resources = {
		minerals = 4
		food = 4
	}
	required_resources = { energy = 5 }
	planet_modifier = {
		slave_mineral_output = 0.15
		slave_food_output = 0.15
		country_unrest_unhappy_slave_effect_mult = -0.60
	}
	potential = {
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
		}
		NOT = {
			tile = { has_building_novus_slave_brainwashing_facility = yes }
		}
	}
	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = "requirement_slave_facility"
			planet = {
				any_pop = { is_enslaved = yes }
			}
		}
	}
	prerequisites = { "tech_novus_neural_brainwashing" }
	ai_allow = {
		NOR = {
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_betharian
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_alien_pets
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_geode_deposit
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_enriched_soil
				amount > 0
			}
		}
		planet = {
			OR = {
				has_building = building_slave_processing
				count_pops = {
					limit = { is_enslaved = yes }
					count > 2
				}
			}
		}
	}
	ai_weight = {
		weight = 1000
		modifier = {
			weight = 0
			from = {
				count_pops = {
					limit = { is_enslaved = yes }
					count < 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	show_tech_unlock_if = { always = no }
	icon = building_novus_slave_brainwashing_facility
	upgrades = { building_slave_processing_hidden_tree_root }
}

					}
				}
			}
		}

				type = sr_novus_geode_deposit

					}
				}
			}
		}

			limit = {
				owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_building_novus_machine_capital_4"

					OR = {
						has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_4"
						has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_5"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

				type = sr_betharian
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_geode_deposit
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {

				amount > 0

	}
	ai_weight = { weight = 5000 }
}

### UNITY BUILDINGS
# Uplink Node
building_uplink_node = {
	base_buildtime = 180
	planet_unique = yes
	cost = { minerals = 100 }
	show_tech_unlock_if = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
	potential = {
		owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
		NAND = {
			owner = { has_technology = "tech_heritage_site" }
			owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_building_capital_1"
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_building = "building_hab_capital"
						has_building_machine_capital_1 = yes
						has_building_machine_capital_2 = yes
						has_building = "building_machine_capital_3"
						has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_4"
						has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_5"
					}
				}
			}
			owner = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = display_low_tier_flag  }
			}
		}
	}
	destroy_if = {
		exists = owner
		owner = {
			NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
		}
	}
	produced_resources = { unity = 2 }
	required_resources = { energy = 1 }
	prerequisites = { "tech_cultural_heritage" }
	upgrades = { building_network_junction }
	ai_allow = {
		NOR = {
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_betharian
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_alien_pets
				amount > 0
			}
		}
	}
	ai_weight = { factor = 1 }
	ai_allow = {
		# If planet only has slaves/robots, keep it to mining and farming...
		is_slave_tile_or_planet = no
	}
}

			owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }

# Alpha Hub
building_alpha_hub = {
	base_buildtime = 720
	is_listed = no
	empire_unique = yes
	cost = { minerals = 500 }
	produced_resources = { unity = 10 }
	required_resources = { energy = 4 }
	country_modifier = { country_resource_unity_mult = 0.10 }
	show_tech_unlock_if = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
	potential = {
		owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
		planet = { is_capital = yes }
	}
	destroy_if = {
		exists = owner
		owner = {
			NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
		}
		planet = { is_capital = no }
	}
	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = "requires_any_empire_capital"
			planet = {
				OR = {
					has_building = "building_machine_capital_3"
					has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_4"
					has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_5"
					has_building = "building_hab_capital"
				}
			}
		}
	}
	prerequisites = { "tech_autocurating_vault" }
	ai_weight = { weight = 20 }
}
### CAPITAL BUILDINGS
building_deployment_post = {
	base_buildtime = 180
	planet_unique = yes
	capital = yes
	level = 0
	defense_armies = 1
	cost = { }
	produced_resources = { energy = 1 }
	produced_resource_trigger = {
		modifier = {
			OR = {
				has_non_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever
				has_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever_machine
				has_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever_hive
			}
			resources = { unity = 1 }
		}
	}
	show_tech_unlock_if = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
	potential = {
		owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
		}
		planet = {
			NOT = {
				has_building = building_deployment_post
				has_building_machine_capital_1 = yes
				has_building_machine_capital_2 = yes
				has_building = building_machine_capital_3
				has_building = building_novus_machine_capital_4
				has_building = building_novus_machine_capital_5
			}
		}
	}
	destroy_if = {
		exists = owner
		owner = {
			NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
		}
	}
	allow = { always = yes }
	upgrades = { building_machine_capital_1 }
	ai_replace = no
}
# Administrative Array
building_machine_capital_1_direct_build = {
	base_buildtime = 360
	planet_unique = yes
	capital = yes
	level = 1
	defense_armies = 3
	cost = { minerals = 350 }
	produced_resources = {
		energy = 4
		unity = 1
	}
	produced_resource_trigger = {
		modifier = {
			OR = {
				has_non_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever
				has_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever_machine
				has_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever_hive
			}
			resources = { unity = 1 }
		}
	}
	adjacency_bonus = {
		tile_building_resource_minerals_add = 1
		tile_building_resource_energy_add = 1
	}
	potential = {
		owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
		}
		NOT = {
			tile = { has_building_machine_capital_1 = yes }
		}
		NAND = {
			owner = { has_technology = "tech_colonial_centralization" }
			owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
			planet = {
				NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_pops_10"
				planet = {
					count_pops = {
						count > 9
						limit = { is_colony_pop = yes }
					}
				}
			}
			owner = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = display_low_tier_flag  }
			}
		}
	}
	destroy_if = {
		exists = owner
		owner = {
			NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
		}
	}
	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = "requires_pops_5"
			planet = {
				count_pops = {
					count > 4
					limit = { is_colony_pop = yes }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	upgrades = { building_machine_capital_2 }
	prerequisites = { "tech_planetary_government" }
	ai_replace = no
	show_tech_unlock_if = { always = no }
	icon = building_machine_capital_1
}

		owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
		}
		NOT = {
			tile = { has_building_machine_capital_2 = yes }
		}
	}
	destroy_if = {
		exists = owner
		owner = {
			NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
		}
	}
	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = "requires_pops_10"
			planet = {
				count_pops = {
					count > 9
					limit = { is_colony_pop = yes }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	planet_unique = yes
	capital = yes
	level = 2
	upgrades = { building_machine_capital_3 }
	prerequisites = { "tech_colonial_centralization" }
	ai_replace = no
	show_tech_unlock_if = { always = no }
	icon = building_machine_capital_2
}

						has_building = "building_machine_capital_3"
						has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_4"

				}
			}

				fail_text = "requires_alien_pets"

# Organic Sanctuary (Servitors Only)
building_organic_sanctuary = {
	is_listed = no
	ai_replace = no
	event_building = yes
	required_resources = { energy = 1 }
	produced_resources = { unity = 1 }
	allow = { always = no }
	destroy_if = {
		exists = owner
		NAND = {
			owner = {
				has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence
				has_government = gov_machine_servitor
			}
			has_grown_pop = yes
			pop = {
				has_living_standard = {
					country = planet.owner
					type = living_standard_organic_trophy
				}
			}
		}
	}
	# Building requires bio-trophy pops to function
	active = {
		# scope: pop
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "bio_trophy_tooltip_1"
			has_living_standard = {
				country = planet.owner
				type = living_standard_organic_trophy
			}
		}
	}
	can_demolish = no
}

	base_buildtime = 360
	planet_unique = yes

	produced_resources = {
		minerals = 2
		energy = 2
	}
	planet_modifier_with_pop_trigger = {
		key = building_neuro_electric_amplifier
		potential = { has_trait = trait_cybernetic }
		modifier = {
			tile_resource_minerals_mult = 0.15
			tile_resource_energy_mult = 0.15
		}
	}
	potential = {
		owner = { has_swapped_tradition = tr_synchronicity_cyber_comms }
	}
	destroy_if = {
		exists = owner
		owner = {
			NOT = {
				has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence
				has_government = gov_machine_assimilator
				has_swapped_tradition = tr_synchronicity_cyber_comms
			}
		}
	}
	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = "requires_building_machine_capital_1"
			planet = {
				OR = {
					has_building_machine_capital_1 = yes
					has_building_machine_capital_2 = yes
					has_building = "building_machine_capital_3"
					has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_4"
					has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_5"
					has_building = "building_hab_capital"
				}
			}
		}
	}
	prerequisites = { }
	ai_allow = {
		NOR = {
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_betharian
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_alien_pets
				amount > 0
			}
		}
		planet = {
			OR = {
				has_building = building_neuro_electric_amplifier
				count_pops = {
					limit = { has_trait = trait_cybernetic }
					count > 2
				}
			}
		}
	}
	ai_weight = { weight = 10 }
}

######################################
# Novus Orbis
# Edited by garvins
######################################
# Do not remove or rename this
# Possible Variables for Buildings:
# strategic_resource: strategic resource, deprecated, strategic resource used by the building.
# allow: trigger to check for allowing construction of building.
# prerequisites: Tech requirements for building.
# empire_unique: boolean, can only build one if set to true.
# cost: resource table, cost of building.
# is_orbital: boolean, can only be built in orbital station.
# modifier: modifier, deprecated, applies a modifier to planet; use planet_modifier instead.
# planet_modifier, country_modifier, army_modifier: applies modifier to planet/country/armies
# triggered_planet_modifier = { key (optional), potential (scope: planet), modifier }: applies conditional modifier to planet
# base_buildtime: int, number of days for construction.
# requires_pop, boolean, building will require a pop for production.
# required_resources, resource table, required resources for production.
# produced_resources, resource table, produced resources in production.
# upgrades, buildings list, buildings this building can upgrade into.
# is_listed, boolean, toggles if this building is shown in the non-upgrade buildable list.
# planet_unique, toggles if one can build multiple of this type on a single planet.
# ai_weight, weight for AI, default is set to one, weight set to 0 means that AI will never build it
# is_colony: trigger to check if the building is a colony shelter for country (scope: country, from: planet). default: "always = no"
# active: trigger to check if a building can be active with a given pop worker (scope: pop) if you add a trigger here, you should also add the requirements in the description
# show_tech_unlock_if: trigger to show this building only conditionally in the technology screen. scope: country. default: { always = yes }
# planet_modifier_with_pop_trigger = { key (optional), potential (scope: pop), modifier }: applies modifier to pops on planet that satisfy condition in trigger
#
# BALANCE
# can change the time and cost of all common buildings with these variables below
########################
### Empire Unique buildings ###
########################
building_galactic_stock_exchange = {
	base_buildtime = 360
	empire_unique = yes
	cost = {
		minerals = 300
		influence = 150
	}
	produced_resources = { energy = 10 }
	show_tech_unlock_if = {
		NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
	}
	potential = {
		NOT = {
			owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
		}
		planet = { is_capital = yes }
	}
	destroy_if = {
		OR = {
			planet = { is_capital = no }
			AND = {
				exists = owner
				owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
			}
		}
	}
	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = "requires_building_capital_2"
			planet = {
				OR = {
					has_building_capital_2 = yes
					has_building_capital_3 = yes
					has_building_novus_capital_4 = yes
					has_building_novus_capital_5 = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	country_modifier = { tile_resource_energy_mult = 0.10 }
	prerequisites = { "tech_galactic_markets" }
	ai_weight = { weight = 20 }
}

	}
	show_tech_unlock_if = {
		NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
	}
	potential = {
		NOT = {
			owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
		}
		planet = { is_capital = yes }
	}
	destroy_if = {
		OR = {
			planet = { is_capital = no }
			AND = {
				exists = owner
				owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
			}
		}
	}
	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = "requires_building_capital_2"
			planet = {
				OR = {
					has_building_capital_2 = yes
					has_building_capital_3 = yes

				}

					fail_text = "requires_betharian_stone"
					tile = {
						has_resource = {
							type = sr_betharian
							amount > 0
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {

			}
			AND = {
				custom_tooltip = {

building_hydroponics_farm_1 = {
	tags = { hydroponics_farm }
	base_buildtime = @b1time
	cost = { minerals = @b1cost }
	produced_resources = { food = 2 }
	produced_resource_trigger = {
		modifier = {
			has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll
			NOT = { has_swapped_tradition = tr_adaptability_finish }
			resources = { unity = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			has_swapped_tradition = tr_adaptability_finish
			NOT = { has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll }
			resources = { minerals = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			has_swapped_tradition = tr_adaptability_finish
			has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll
			resources = {
				unity = 1
				minerals = 1
			}
		}
	}
	required_resources = { energy = @b1upkeep }
	upgrades = { building_hydroponics_farm_2 }
	prerequisites = { "tech_eco_simulation" }
	show_tech_unlock_if = {
		NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
	}
	potential = {
		NOT = {
			owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
		}
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
		}
		NAND = {
			owner = { has_technology = "tech_hydroponics" }
			NOT = {
				owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
			}
			planet = {
				NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_building_capital_1"
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_building_capital_1 = yes
						has_building_capital_2 = yes
						has_building_capital_3 = yes
						has_building_novus_capital_4 = yes
						has_building_novus_capital_5 = yes
					}
				}
			}
			owner = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = display_low_tier_flag  }
			}
		}
	}
	destroy_if = {
		exists = owner
		owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
	}
	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = "requires_building_capital_1"
			planet = {
				OR = {
					has_building_capital_1 = yes
					has_building_capital_2 = yes
					has_building_capital_3 = yes
					has_building_novus_capital_4 = yes
					has_building_novus_capital_5 = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	ai_allow = {
		NOR = {
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_betharian
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_alien_pets
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_geode_deposit
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_enriched_soil
				amount > 0
			}
		}
	}
	ai_weight = { factor = 1 }
}

building_mining_network_1 = {
	tags = { mining_network }
	base_buildtime = @b1time
	potential = {
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
		}
		NAND = {
			owner = { has_technology = "tech_mining_network_2" }
			planet = {
				NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = "requires_building_capital_1"
					planet = {
						OR = {
							has_building_capital_1 = yes
							has_building_capital_2 = yes
							has_building_capital_3 = yes
							has_building_novus_capital_4 = yes
							has_building_novus_capital_5 = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
				}
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = "requires_building_machine_capital_1"
					planet = {
						OR = {
							has_building_machine_capital_1 = yes
							has_building_machine_capital_2 = yes
							has_building = "building_machine_capital_3"
							has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_4"
							has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_5"
						}
					}
				}
			}
			owner = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = display_low_tier_flag  }
			}
		}
	}
	cost = { minerals = @b1cost }
	produced_resources = { minerals = 2 }
	required_resources = { energy = @b1upkeep }
	upgrades = { building_mining_network_2 }
	prerequisites = { "tech_basic_industry" }
	ai_allow = {
		NOR = {
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_betharian
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_alien_pets
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_geode_deposit
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_enriched_soil
				amount > 0
			}
		}
	}
	ai_weight = { factor = 1 }
}

				}
			}

				text = "requires_building_capital_2"
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_building_capital_2 = yes
						has_building_capital_3 = yes
						has_building_novus_capital_4 = yes
						has_building_novus_capital_5 = yes
						has_building = "building_hab_capital"
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_building_machine_capital_2"
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_building_machine_capital_2 = yes
						has_building = "building_machine_capital_3"
						has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_4"
						has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_5"
						has_building = "building_hab_capital"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	planet_modifier = { static_planet_resource_minerals_add = 30 }
	required_resources = { energy = 50 }
	prerequisites = { "tech_matter_generator" }
	ai_replace = no
	ai_weight = { factor = 0 }
}

							has_building_capital_3 = yes
							has_building_novus_capital_4 = yes
							has_building_novus_capital_5 = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
				}
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = "requires_building_machine_capital_1"
					planet = {
						OR = {
							has_building_machine_capital_1 = yes
							has_building_machine_capital_2 = yes
							has_building = "building_machine_capital_3"
							has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_4"
							has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_5"
						}
					}
				}
			}
			owner = { has_technology = "tech_physics_lab_1" }
			owner = { has_technology = "tech_biolab_1" }
			owner = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = display_low_tier_flag  }
			}
		}
	}
	produced_resources = {
		engineering_research = @science1
		physics_research = @science1
		society_research = @science1
	}
	required_resources = { energy = @b1upkeep }
	upgrades = {
		building_engineering_facility_1
		building_physics_lab_1
		building_biolab_1
	}
	prerequisites = { "tech_basic_science_lab_1" }
	ai_allow = {
		NOR = {
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_betharian
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_alien_pets
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_geode_deposit
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_enriched_soil
				amount > 0
			}
		}
		# If planet only has slaves/robots, keep it to mining and farming...
		is_slave_tile_or_planet = no
	}
	ai_weight = { factor = 1 }
}

						has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_4"
						has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_5"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	produced_resources = {
		engineering_research = @science1
		physics_research = @science2
		society_research = @science1
	}
	required_resources = { energy = @b2upkeep }
	upgrades = { building_physics_lab_2 }
	prerequisites = { "tech_physics_lab_1" }
	ai_allow = {
		NOR = {
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_betharian
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_alien_pets
				amount > 0

				amount > 0

			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_enriched_soil
				amount > 0
			}
		}

		is_slave_tile_or_planet = no
	}
	show_tech_unlock_if = { always = no }
	icon = building_physics_lab_1
}

	is_listed = no

			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
		}
	}

					NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_building_capital_1"
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_building_capital_1 = yes
						has_building_capital_2 = yes
						has_building_capital_3 = yes
						has_building_novus_capital_4 = yes
						has_building_novus_capital_5 = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}

				text = "requires_building_machine_capital_1"
				planet = {

						has_building_machine_capital_1 = yes
						has_building_machine_capital_2 = yes
						has_building = "building_machine_capital_3"
						has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_4"

		}

							has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_5"
						}
					}
				}
			}
			owner = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = display_low_tier_flag  }
			}
		}
	}
	allow = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_building_capital_2"
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_building_capital_2 = yes
						has_building_capital_3 = yes
						has_building_novus_capital_4 = yes
						has_building_novus_capital_5 = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_building_machine_capital_2"
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_building_machine_capital_2 = yes
						has_building = "building_machine_capital_3"
						has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_4"
						has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_5"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	produced_resources = {
		engineering_research = @science1
		physics_research = @science1
		society_research = @science3
	}
	required_resources = { energy = @b3upkeep }
	upgrades = { building_biolab_3 }
	prerequisites = { "tech_biolab_2" }
	ai_allow = {
		NOR = {
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_betharian
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_alien_pets
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_geode_deposit
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_enriched_soil
				amount > 0
			}
		}
		# If planet only has slaves/robots, keep it to mining and farming...
		is_slave_tile_or_planet = no
	}
	show_tech_unlock_if = { always = no }
	icon = building_biolab_2

building_autochthon_monument = {
	base_buildtime = 180
	planet_unique = yes
	cost = { minerals = 100 }
	show_tech_unlock_if = {
		NOR = {
			has_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
			has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence
		}
	}
	potential = {
		owner = {
			NOR = {
				has_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
				has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence
			}
		}
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			NOR = {
				has_building = building_temple
				has_building_holotemple = yes
				has_building = building_citadel_of_faith
				has_building_sacred_nexus = yes
			}
		}
		NAND = {
			owner = { has_technology = "tech_heritage_site" }
			owner = {
				NOR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
					has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence
				}
			}
			planet = {
				NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
				NOR = {
					has_building = building_temple
					has_building_holotemple = yes
					has_building = building_citadel_of_faith
					has_building_sacred_nexus = yes
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_building_capital_1"
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_building_capital_1 = yes
						has_building_capital_2 = yes
						has_building_capital_3 = yes
						has_building_novus_capital_4 = yes
						has_building_novus_capital_5 = yes
					}
				}
			}
			owner = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = display_low_tier_flag  }
			}
		}
	}
	destroy_if = {
		exists = owner
		owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
	}
	produced_resources = { unity = 2 }
	required_resources = { energy = 1 }
	prerequisites = { "tech_cultural_heritage" }
	upgrades = { building_heritage_site }
	ai_allow = {
		NOR = {
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_betharian
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_alien_pets
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_geode_deposit
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_enriched_soil
				amount > 0
			}
		}
	}
	ai_weight = { factor = 1 }
	ai_allow = {
		# If planet only has slaves/robots, keep it to mining and farming...
		is_slave_tile_or_planet = no
	}
}

	planet_modifier = { pop_ethic_spiritualist_attraction_mult = 0.2 }
	prerequisites = { "tech_cultural_heritage" }
	required_resources = { energy = 1 }
	show_tech_unlock_if = {
		OR = {
			has_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
		}
	}
	potential = {
		owner = {
			OR = {
				has_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
			}
		}
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			NOR = {
				has_building = building_autochthon_monument
				has_building_heritage_site = yes
				has_building_hypercomms_forum = yes
				has_building = building_autocurating_vault
			}
		}
		NAND = {
			owner = { has_technology = "tech_holographic_rituals" }
			owner = {
				OR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
				}
			}
			planet = {
				NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
				NOR = {
					has_building = building_autochthon_monument
					has_building_heritage_site = yes
					has_building_hypercomms_forum = yes
					has_building = building_autocurating_vault
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_building_capital_1"
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_building_capital_1 = yes
						has_building_capital_2 = yes
						has_building_capital_3 = yes
						has_building_novus_capital_4 = yes
						has_building_novus_capital_5 = yes
					}
				}
			}
			owner = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = display_low_tier_flag  }
			}
		}
	}
	destroy_if = {
		exists = owner
		owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
	}
	upgrades = { building_holotemple }
	ai_allow = {
		NOR = {
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_betharian
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_alien_pets
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_geode_deposit
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_enriched_soil
				amount > 0
			}
		}
	}
	ai_weight = { factor = 10 }
	ai_allow = {
		# If planet only has slaves/robots, keep it to mining and farming...
		is_slave_tile_or_planet = no
	}
}

	base_buildtime = 180
	planet_unique = yes
	capital = yes
	level = 0
	defense_armies = 1
	cost = { }
	produced_resources = { energy = 1 }
	produced_resource_trigger = {
		modifier = {
			OR = {
				has_non_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever
				has_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever_machine
				has_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever_hive
			}
			resources = { unity = 1 }
		}
	}
	planet_modifier = { pop_government_ethic_attraction = 0.05 }
	show_tech_unlock_if = {
		NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
	}
	potential = {
		NOT = {
			owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
		}
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
		}
		planet = {
			NOT = {
				has_building = building_colony_shelter
				has_building_capital_1 = yes
				has_building_capital_2 = yes
				has_building_capital_3 = yes
			}
		}
	}
	destroy_if = {
		exists = owner
		owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
	}
	upgrades = { building_capital_1 }
	ai_replace = no
}

building_capital_1_direct_build = {
	base_buildtime = 360
	planet_unique = yes
	capital = yes
	level = 1
	defense_armies = 3
	cost = { minerals = 350 }
	produced_resources = {
		energy = 4
		unity = 1
	}
	produced_resource_trigger = {
		modifier = {
			OR = {
				has_non_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever
				has_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever_machine
				has_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever_hive
			}
			resources = { unity = 1 }
		}
	}
	adjacency_bonus = {
		tile_building_resource_minerals_add = 1
		tile_building_resource_food_add = 1
		tile_building_resource_energy_add = 1
	}
	planet_modifier = { pop_government_ethic_attraction = 0.15 }
	potential = {
		NOT = {
			owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
		}
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
		}
		NOT = {
			tile = { has_building_capital_1 = yes }
		}
		NAND = {
			owner = { has_technology = "tech_colonial_centralization" }
			NOT = {
				owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
			}
			planet = {
				NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_pops_10"
				planet = {
					count_pops = {
						count > 9
						limit = { is_colony_pop = yes }
					}
				}
			}
			owner = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = display_low_tier_flag  }
			}
		}
	}
	destroy_if = {
		exists = owner
		owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
	}
	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = "requires_pops_5"
			planet = {
				count_pops = {
					count > 4
					limit = { is_colony_pop = yes }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	upgrades = { building_capital_2 }
	prerequisites = { "tech_planetary_government" }
	ai_replace = no
	show_tech_unlock_if = { always = no }
	icon = building_capital_1
}

			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
		}
	}
	destroy_if = {
		exists = owner
		owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
	}
	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = "requires_pops_15"
			planet = {
				count_pops = {
					count > 14
					limit = { is_colony_pop = yes }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	upgrades = { building_novus_capital_4 }
	prerequisites = { "tech_galactic_administration" }
	ai_replace = no
}
# Clone Vats are required to build Clone Armies
building_clone_vats = {
	base_buildtime = 360
	planet_unique = yes
	cost = { minerals = 200 }
	produced_resources = { society_research = 4 }
	required_resources = { energy = 2 }
	potential = {
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
		}
	}
	allow = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_building_capital_2"
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_building_capital_2 = yes
						has_building_capital_3 = yes
						has_building_novus_capital_4 = yes
						has_building_novus_capital_5 = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_building_machine_capital_2"
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_building_machine_capital_2 = yes
						has_building = "building_machine_capital_3"
						has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_4"
						has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_5"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	prerequisites = { "tech_gene_banks" }
	ai_allow = {
		NOR = {
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_betharian
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_alien_pets
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_geode_deposit
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_enriched_soil
				amount > 0
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			planet = {
				owner = {
					any_owned_planet = {
						NOT = { is_same_value = from }
						has_building = building_clone_vats
					}
				}
			}
		}
		# If planet only has slaves/robots, keep it to mining and farming...
		is_slave_tile_or_planet = no
	}
	ai_weight = {
		weight = 10
		modifier = {
			weight = 0
			from = {
				owner = {
					NOT = {
						has_technology = tech_gene_banks
						OR = {
							has_ethic = ethic_militarist
							has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_militarist
						}
					}
				}
				NOT = { has_building = building_clone_vats }
			}
		}
	}
}

	potential = { always = no }
	planet_unique = yes
	icon = building_slave_processing
}
building_slave_processing = {
	base_buildtime = 360
	planet_unique = yes
	cost = { minerals = 250 }
	produced_resources = {
		minerals = 2
		food = 2
	}
	required_resources = { energy = 3 }
	planet_modifier = {
		slave_mineral_output = 0.10
		slave_food_output = 0.10
		country_unrest_unhappy_slave_effect_mult = -0.25
	}
	show_tech_unlock_if = {
		NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
	}
	potential = {
		NOT = {
			owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
		}
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
		}
		NAND = {
			owner = { has_technology = "tech_novus_neural_brainwashing" }
			planet = {
				NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requirement_slave_facility"
				planet = {
					any_pop = { is_enslaved = yes }
				}
			}
			owner = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = display_low_tier_flag  }
			}
		}
	}
	destroy_if = {
		exists = owner
		owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
	}
	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = "requirement_slave_facility"
			planet = {
				any_pop = { is_enslaved = yes }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_building_capital_1"
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_building_capital_1 = yes
						has_building_capital_2 = yes
						has_building_capital_3 = yes
						has_building_novus_capital_4 = yes
						has_building_novus_capital_5 = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_building_machine_capital_1"
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_building_machine_capital_1 = yes
						has_building_machine_capital_2 = yes
						has_building = "building_machine_capital_3"
						has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_4"
						has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_5"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	prerequisites = { "tech_neural_implants" }
	upgrades = { building_novus_slave_brainwashing_facility }
	ai_allow = {
		NOR = {
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_betharian
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_alien_pets
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_geode_deposit
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_novus_enriched_soil
				amount > 0
			}
		}
		planet = {
			OR = {
				has_building = building_slave_processing
				count_pops = {
					limit = { is_enslaved = yes }
					count > 2
				}
			}
		}
	}
	ai_weight = { weight = 10 }
}

building_stronghold = {
	base_buildtime = 180
	is_listed = yes
	defense_armies = 3
	protects_from_bombardment = yes
	planetary_ftl_inhibitor = yes
	prerequisites = { "tech_planetary_defenses" }
	cost = { minerals = 300 }
	produced_resources = { unity = 1 }
	required_resources = { energy = 2 }
	upgrades = { building_fortress }
	planet_modifier = { planet_unrest_add = -30 }
	ai_weight = {
		weight = 1000
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			years_passed < 25
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			planet = {
				NOR = {
					unrest > 50
					AND = {
						planet_size > 12
						OR = {
							has_building_capital_1 = yes
							has_building_capital_2 = yes
							has_building_capital_3 = yes
							has_building_novus_capital_4 = yes
							has_building_novus_capital_5 = yes
							has_building_machine_capital_1 = yes
							has_building_machine_capital_2 = yes
							has_building = "building_machine_capital_3"
							has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_4"
							has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_5"
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			planet = {
				NOR = {
					unrest > 50
					AND = {
						planet_size > 16
						OR = {
							has_building_capital_2 = yes
							has_building_capital_3 = yes
							has_building_novus_capital_4 = yes
							has_building_novus_capital_5 = yes
							has_building_machine_capital_2 = yes
							has_building = "building_machine_capital_3"
							has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_4"
							has_building = "building_novus_machine_capital_5"
						}
					}
				}
				count_tile = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_building = building_stronghold
